function uid(){return "00000000000000000000000000000000".replace(/0/g,function(){return(0|Math.random()*16).toString(16)})};

function unique(array,prop){
    var flags = [], output = [], l = array.length, i;
    for( i=0; i<l; i++) {
        if( flags[array[i][prop]]) continue;
        flags[array[i][prop]] = true;
        output.push(array[i]);
    }
    return output
}

function hintergrundcover(t){
    imagesLoaded(t,function(){ 
        var r = t.naturalWidth / t.naturalHeight; 
    var g = r < window.innerWidth / window.innerHeight; 
    t.style.width =  g ? "100%" : "auto"; 
    t.style.height =  g ?  "auto" : "100%"; 
    t.style.left = g ? "0" : (window.innerWidth - t.width) / 2 + "px"; 
    t.style.top = g ? (window.innerHeight - t.height) / 2 + "px" : "0"; })
}

function leaflet(k){ 
	//map.remove()
	lmap = new L.map('map');
	lmap.setView([51.48566, 11.96866], 14);
    var pin = L.icon({
        iconUrl: 'http://buehnen-halle.de/img/leaflet/bh-pin.png',
        shadowUrl: 'http://buehnen-halle.de/img/leaflet/bh-pin_schatten.png',
        iconSize:     [38, 70],
        shadowSize:   [59, 21],
        iconAnchor:   [12, 70],
        shadowAnchor: [12, 21],
        popupAnchor:  [5, -10]
    });
    L.tileLayer('http://server.arcgisonline.com/ArcGIS/rest/services/World_Topo_Map/MapServer/tile/{z}/{y}/{x}', {
    maxZoom: 18
    }).addTo(lmap);
    if(k=="too"){
        L.marker([51.4855, 11.96881],{icon:pin}).addTo(lmap).bindPopup("Kulturinsel (neues theater, Thalia Theater, Puppentheater)");
        L.marker([51.48665, 11.97112],{icon:pin}).addTo(lmap).bindPopup("Oper"); }
    if(k=="weitere"){
        L.marker([51.486445, 11.969290],{icon:pin}).addTo(lmap).bindPopup("Aula der Universität");
        L.marker([51.481800, 11.964272],{icon:pin}).addTo(lmap).bindPopup("Georg-Friedrich-Händel HALLE");
        L.marker([51.484108, 11.966874],{icon:pin}).addTo(lmap).bindPopup("Händel-Haus");
        L.marker([51.488371, 11.977418],{icon:pin}).addTo(lmap).bindPopup("Historischer Hörsaal im Anatomischen Institut");
        L.marker([51.478337, 11.978123],{icon:pin}).addTo(lmap).bindPopup("Kongress- und Kulturzentrum");
        L.marker([51.482491, 11.968109],{icon:pin}).addTo(lmap).bindPopup("Marktkirche Unser Lieben Frauen");
        L.marker([51.496043, 11.971284],{icon:pin}).addTo(lmap).bindPopup("Pauluskirche");
        L.marker([51.496907, 11.955822],{icon:pin}).addTo(lmap).bindPopup("Volkspark"); }
    if(k=="kulturinsel"){
        L.marker([51.4855, 11.96881],{icon:pin}).addTo(lmap).bindPopup("Kulturinsel (neues theater, Thalia Theater, Puppentheater)");}
    if(k=="oper"){
        L.marker([51.48665, 11.97112],{icon:pin}).addTo(lmap).bindPopup("Oper");}
    
    var popup = L.popup();
    function onMapClick(e) { popup.setLatLng(e.latlng).setContent(e.latlng.toString()).openOn(lmap); }
    lmap.on('contextmenu', onMapClick);    
}

function anyMatchInArray(target, toMatch) {
    var found, targetMap, i, j, cur;
    found = false;
    targetMap = {};
    for (i = 0, j = target.length; i < j; i++) {
        cur = target[i];
        targetMap[cur] = true;
    }
    for (i = 0, j = toMatch.length; !found && (i < j); i++) {
        cur = toMatch[i];
        found = !!targetMap[cur];
    }
    return found;
}

var mobilenavopen = false;
var animatenav = function(speed){
   Velocity(document.getElementById("mobilenav"),{ translateX: mobilenavopen ? ["100%","0"] : ["0","100%"]}, speed, [ 150, 40 ]);
   Velocity(document.getElementById("open"), { opacity: mobilenavopen ? [1,0] : [0,1] },  speed, {queue:false});
   Velocity(document.getElementById("close"), { opacity: mobilenavopen ? [0,1] : [1,0] }, speed, function(){mobilenavopen = !mobilenavopen;});    
   }   
 
   window.$ = function(selector, el) {
      var element = !!el ? el : document;
      return element.querySelector(selector);
    };

    window.$$ = function(selector, el) {
      var items = {},
      results = [],
      length = 0,
      i = 0,
      element = !!el ? el : document;
      results = Array.prototype.slice.call(element.querySelectorAll(selector));
      length = results.length;
      for ( ; i < length; ) {
        items[i] = results[i];
        i++;
      }
      items.length = length;
      items.splice = [].splice();
      items.each = function(callback) {
        var i = 0;
        for ( ; i < length; ) {
          callback.call(items[i]);
          i++;
        }
      }
      return items;
    };



   function scriptload(scr){
       var jsTag = document.createElement('script');
       jsTag.type = "text/javascript";
       jsTag.src = 'scr';
       document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(jsTag);
   }

   var md = window.markdownit({html:true,xhtmlOut:true}).use(window.markdownItAttrs);

   Array.min = function(array) {
       return Math.min.apply(Math, array);
   };
   Array.max = function(array) {
       return Math.max.apply(Math, array);
   };

   var forEach = function (array, callback, scope) {
     for (var i = 0; i < array.length; i++) {
       callback.call(scope, i, array[i]); 
     }
   };

   var didScroll = false;
   //var oben = verge.scrollY() < heights[0] - window.innerHeight;
   var scroll = function () {
       if($$(".hintergrund")[0]) {
  	 if(verge.scrollY() > heights[0] - window.innerHeight - 16) {$$(".hintergrund")[0].style.webkitFilter="brightness(100%)"; $$(".hintergrund")[0].style.webkitFilter="brightness(100%)";}
       else {$$(".hintergrund")[0].style.webkitFilter="brightness(50%)"; $$(".hintergrund")[0].style.webkitFilter="brightness(50%)";}
   }
   };

   var raf = window.requestAnimationFrame || window.webkitRequestAnimationFrame || window.mozRequestAnimationFrame || window.msRequestAnimationFrame || window.oRequestAnimationFrame;
   var lastScrollTop = verge.scrollY();
   if (raf) {
       loop();
   }
   function loop() {
       var scrollTop = verge.scrollY();
       if (lastScrollTop === scrollTop) {
           raf(loop);
           return;
       } else {
           lastScrollTop = scrollTop;
           scroll();
           raf(loop);
       }
   }
 
  var colCount = 0;
  var colWidth = 150;
  var margin = 10;
  var spaceLeft = 0;
  var Width = 0;
  var heights;

  window.onresize = setupBlocks;

  function setupBlocks() {
  	heights = [];
      Width = window.innerWidth;
  	colCount = Math.floor(Width/(colWidth+2*margin));
  	spaceLeft = (Width - (colWidth * Math.max(colCount,2) + margin * colCount)) / 2 - margin / (colCount + 1)	
  	if(!!$$(".hintergrund")[0]) hintergrundcover($$(".hintergrund")[0])
    for(var i=0;i<colCount;i++){ heights.push(margin); }
    if($("#footer")) $("#footer").style.height = window.innerHeight + 20 + "px";
  	var blocks = document.querySelectorAll('.block');
      for(i=0;i<blocks.length;i++){
          var wvorhanden = blocks[i].className.match(/(^| )w(\d)( |$)/); 
          var mvorhanden = blocks[i].className.match(/(^| )m(\d)( |$)/); 
          var cols = colCount > 1 ? (!!mvorhanden ? colCount - mvorhanden[2] : !!wvorhanden ? Math.min(wvorhanden[2], Math.floor(window.innerWidth / 180)) : 1 ) : 1; 
          var tmpheights = cols > 1 ? mehrspaltige(cols) : heights;
          var min = tmpheights.length ? Array.min(tmpheights) : 0;
  		var index = tmpheights.indexOf(min);
  		var leftPos = margin+(index*(colWidth+margin)); 
          if(!!mvorhanden) blocks[i].style.width = (Math.max(colCount,2) * (colWidth + margin) - margin) + 'px';
          blocks[i].style.display = "block";
          blocks[i].style.position = "absolute";
          blocks[i].style.left = (leftPos+spaceLeft)+'px';
  	    blocks[i].style.top = min+'px'; 
          $$("iframe", blocks[i]).each(function() {
              var h=this.height; 
              var w=this.width; 
              this.width = this.parentNode.offsetWidth; 
              this.height = Math.floor( h / w *  this.parentNode.offsetWidth );             
          });
          for(j=1;j<=cols;j++) { heights[index + j - 1] = min + blocks[i].offsetHeight + margin;  }
  	}	      
  }

  var mehrspaltige = function(spalten){
      return heights.map(function(e,i,a){return Array.max(heights.slice(i,i+spalten))}).slice(0,-(spalten-1))
  }
  
  var layout = function(){
      $$(".kaestchen a, .monatslinks a",$("blocks")).each(function(){
          var el = this;
                  
          if(!el.getAttribute("linked")){
          el.setAttribute("linked",true);
          var href = this.getAttribute("href");
              if(/^#[^\!]/.test(href)) { 
  			this.addEventListener('click', function (e) { 
                  e.preventDefault(); 
                
                  Velocity($(el.getAttribute('href')),"scroll",{duration:1000}); 
                  Velocity(document.getElementsByName(el.getAttribute('href').replace(/^#/,""))[0],"scroll",{duration:1000}); });
  		}
          if(/\.jpg|png|gif/i.test(href)){
          	var el=this; 
  			app.bilderstrecke(app.bilderstrecke().concat([href]))
            el.addEventListener('click', function (event) { 
                event.preventDefault();
                for(i=0;i<app.bilderstrecke().length;i++){if(app.bilderstrecke()[i].replace(/.*\//,"") == event.target.getAttribute("src").replace(/.*\//,"")) {galerie.aktuell=i; break;} }
                app.galeriesichtbar(true);                     
                m.redraw();  
                });
          }
  		if(!/ical/.test(href) && !/^#/.test(href) && !/^mailto/i.test(href) && !/^https?:\/\//.test(href) && !/\.jpg|zip|png|gif/i.test(href) && !/\.pdf/i.test(href))
              { el.addEventListener('click', function (e) { e.preventDefault(); m.route.set(el.getAttribute('href'));  });}
          }});
      if(app.doc() && app.doc().slug == "start") try {twttr.ready(function (twttr) { twttr.widgets.load();})} catch(e){} 
      setupBlocks(); 
      if(!!document.getElementById('blocks')) imagesLoaded( document.getElementById('blocks'), function() { setupBlocks() }) 
      if($("#map") && !$("#map").getAttribute("linked")) {leaflet($("#map").getAttribute("rel")); $("#map").setAttribute("linked",true)}    
        
  }

function spielplanmonateweise(spielplan){
    var monate = [];
    var tage = [];
    var tag = [];
    spielplan.forEach(function(t,i,s){ 
        if(!s[i-1]) tag.push(t)
        else { 
            if(t.datum.substr(0,10) != s[i-1]["datum"].substr(0,10)) { 
                tage.push(tag); 
                tag = []; 
                } 
            if(t.datum.substr(0,7) != s[i-1]["datum"].substr(0,7)) { 
                monate.push(tage); 
                tage = []; 
                } 
             tag.push(t); 
             if(!s[i+1]) {
                 tage.push(tag);
                 monate.push(tage);
             }
             }                    
    });
    return monate                        
    }

var galerie = {
	aktuell: 0,
	dreierkette : [],
	vorzuladen: {},
    velocity_is_running : false,
    auto: false,
    weg: function(){galerie.auto = false; clearTimeout(galerie.automatisch);	app.galeriesichtbar(false); m.redraw();},
	swiping: function(richtung){ 
		if(!!richtung) galerie.vorzuladen = app.bilderstrecke()[(galerie.aktuell +  richtung * 3 + app.bilderstrecke().length) % app.bilderstrecke().length];
		Velocity(galerie.is_panning.querySelectorAll(".bild"), {left: function(i){ return (i - richtung - 1)*galerie.width}}, {
	        duration: galerie.width/2,
			easing: "easeInOutCubic",
	        begin: function(){ galerie.velocity_is_running = true; },
			complete: function() {			
				galerie.velocity_is_running = false;
				if(richtung) {
					[].forEach.call(galerie.is_panning.querySelectorAll("img"), function(bild, i){
						bild.addEventListener('dragstart',function(event){ event.preventDefault() });
					});	
					if(richtung < 0) {galerie.dreierkette.unshift(app.bilderstrecke()[(galerie.aktuell + richtung - 1 + 2 *  app.bilderstrecke().length)%app.bilderstrecke().length]);galerie.dreierkette.pop();}
					else {galerie.dreierkette.push(app.bilderstrecke()[(galerie.aktuell+richtung+1+app.bilderstrecke().length)%app.bilderstrecke().length]);galerie.dreierkette.shift();}			
                    m.redraw()
					galerie.aktuell = (galerie.aktuell + richtung) % app.bilderstrecke().length;
					if(galerie.auto)  galerie.automatisch = setTimeout(function(){galerie.swiping(1);},8000);
                 
				}
			}
	    })	
	},	    

	hammertime_init : function(vnode){
		galerie.auto = true
        galerie.velocity_is_running = false;
		galerie.is_panning = vnode.dom;
		window.addEventListener('keydown', function (e){
			 if(!galerie.velocity_is_running && [37,39].indexOf(e.keyCode) != -1) {
				 galerie.auto = false; 
				 clearTimeout(galerie.automatisch); 
				 galerie.swiping(e.keyCode-38);
			 }
             if(e.keyCode == 27) galerie.weg()
		 });
		[].forEach.call(vnode.dom.querySelectorAll("img"), function(bild, i){
			bild.addEventListener('dragstart',function(event){ event.preventDefault() });
		});
		galerie.width = vnode.dom.parentNode.offsetWidth;		
		galerie.hammertime = new Hammer(vnode.dom);		
		galerie.hammertime.on('pan', function(ev) {
            galerie.auto = false;	
			clearTimeout(galerie.automatisch); 
		
            if(!galerie.velocity_is_running) 
				[].forEach.call(vnode.dom.querySelectorAll(".bild"), function(elem, i){
					elem.style.left = ev.deltaX + (i-1) * galerie.width + "px";
				});		
		});
		galerie.hammertime.on("press", {time:30}, function(ev) {		    
            galerie.auto = false;	
			clearTimeout(galerie.automatisch);	
		});
		galerie.hammertime.on('panend', function(ev) {
            var richtung = Math.abs(ev.velocityX) > 0.4 && ev.distance > 10 ? ev.direction-3 : ev.deltaX > 0 ? ev.deltaX > galerie.width/2 ? 1 : 0 : ev.deltaX < -galerie.width/2 ? -1 : 0;			
			galerie.swiping(-richtung);
		});
		galerie.automatisch = setTimeout(function(){galerie.swiping(1);},8000);
	},

	stepright :function(){ galerie.auto = false;  clearTimeout(galerie.automatisch); galerie.swiping(1);},
	stepleft : function(){ galerie.auto = false;  clearTimeout(galerie.automatisch); galerie.swiping(-1);},

    oninit: function(vnode) {
		galerie.dreierkette = [app.bilderstrecke()[app.bilderstrecke().length - 1], app.bilderstrecke()[galerie.aktuell], app.bilderstrecke()[galerie.aktuell + 1]];	
	
	
	},

	view: function() {
		return [
			m("#step_left",{onclick:galerie.stepleft},m.trust("<svg xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg version='1.1'  height='2em' viewBox='0 0 100 100' width='2em'><polyline fill='none' stroke='#fff' stroke-width='12' stroke-linejoin='miter' stroke-miterlimit='2' points='50,90 50,10 10,50 50,10 90,50' transform='rotate(270,50,50)'></polyline></svg>")),
			m("#step_right",{onclick:galerie.stepright},m.trust("<svg xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg version='1.1'  height='2em' viewBox='0 0 100 100' width='2em'><polyline fill='none' stroke='#fff' stroke-width='12' stroke-linejoin='miter' stroke-miterlimit='2' points='50,90 50,10 10,50 50,10 90,50' transform='rotate(90,50,50)'></polyline></svg>")),
			
            m("#vorladecontainer", galerie.vorzuladen ? m("img",{ src: "http://buehnen-halle.de" + galerie.vorzuladen}) : null),
			m(".dreierkette", {oncreate:galerie.hammertime_init},
			galerie.dreierkette.map(function(item,i){return m(".bild",{style: "left:" + ((i-1)*100) + "%", key:item}, m(".zentrier_container",  m(".inhalt" , [m("img",{ src: "http://buehnen-halle.de" + item})] )))})),
            m("#x",{ onclick: galerie.weg }, "×"),				
			]
		
	
		
		}
	}

             		                                               t.slug != "kein" && !t.kein_link  ? m('a[href="/' + t.slug + '"]', { class:sparte2linkfarbe[t.kunstgattung.split(",")[0]], oncreate : m.route.link }, m.trust(t.titel)) : t.kein_link ? m("span", {class:sparte2linkfarbe[t.kunstgattung.split(",")[0]],style:"font-weight:800"}, m.trust(t.titel)) : m("strong.undefined", m.trust(t.titel)), m.trust("&emsp;")," ",
             		                                                (t.kunstgattung.split(",").indexOf("99")  != -1 && false) || t.flag == "X" || t.keinkartenbutton ? null 
                                                                        : t.status == "0" && !(t.flag == "T" || t.flag == "G" || t.flag == "R" || t.flag == "A" || t.flag == "W" || t.flag == "F" || t.flag =="K" || t.flag =="S") ? 
                                                                            m("span.karten",{style:"letter-spacing:0;"},"AUSVERKAUFT (evtl. Restkarten an der Abendkasse)") 
                                                                        : t.flag == "A"  && (new XDate()).toISOString() < "2017-07-01T09" ? 
                                                                            m("span.karten",{style:"letter-spacing:0;"},"Karten ab 1.7.2017") 
                                                                        : t.flag == "Y" ? 
                                                                            m("span.karten",{style:"letter-spacing:0;"},"Karten ab 25.7.2017") 
                                                                        : t.flag == "R" ? 
                                                                            m("span.karten",{style:"letter-spacing:0;"},"Restkarten an der Theater- und Konzertkasse") 
                                                                        : t.flag == "T" ? 
                                                                            m("span.karten",{style:"letter-spacing:0;"},"Karten vor Ort oder an der Theaterkasse") 
                                                                        : t.flag == "K" ? 
                                                                            m("span.karten",{style:"letter-spacing:0;"},"Eintritt frei") 
                                                                        : t.flag == "S" ? 
                                                                            m("span.karten",{style:"letter-spacing:0;"},"Eintritt bei Austritt") 
                                                                        : t.flag == "F" ? 
                                                                            m("span.karten",{class:"ausverkauft", style:"letter-spacing:0;"},"AUSVERKAUFT (evtl. Restkarten an der Abendkasse)") 
                                                                        : t.flag == "G" ? 
                                                                            m("span.karten",{style:"letter-spacing:0;"},"externer Kartenverkauf") 
                                                                        : t.flag == "L" && t.kunstgattung.split(",").indexOf("9") == -1  ?
                                                                            m('a.karten[href="http://www.goethe-theater-bad-lauchstaedt.de/ticket-service.html"]',"Karten ↗")
                                                                        : t.flag == "W" && t.kunstgattung.split(",").indexOf("9") == -1  ?
                                                                            m('a.karten[href="http://www.kurt-weill.de/shop/start.html"]',"Karten ↗")
                                                                        : m('a.karten[href="http://tickets.buehnen-halle.de/eventim.webshop/webticket/shop?event=' + t.eventim_veranstaltungs_id + '"]', {target:"_new"}, t.status == "1" ? "RESTKARTEN" : "KARTEN"), !!t.kurzuntertitel ? m(".ut",m.trust(t.kurzuntertitel)) : null
                                                             ])
             		                                            ]) // .termin

             	                                            }))
             	                                        ]) // Tag
             	                                    }))
                                             }) : "Lädt") : null,
        ]),
        m(mobilenav),
        m(trigger),
        app.galeriesichtbar() ? m(galerie) : null,
        m(modal),
        
        !!app.sparte() && hintergruende[app.sparte()] ? m(".block.m0[id='footer']", [m("div",m("b", hintergruende[app.sparte()][0]["bu"]))]) : m(".block.m0[id='minifooter']")

    ///////////////
        
        
    ///////////////
    
        ]) : false ? m(".loading-icon",m.trust('<svg width="120px" height="120px" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 100 100" preserveAspectRatio="xMidYMid" class="uil-gear"><rect x="0" y="0" width="100" height="100" fill="none" class="bk"></rect><path d="M75,50.5l5-1.5c-0.1-2.2-0.4-4.3-0.9-6.3l-5.2-0.1c-0.2-0.6-0.4-1.1-0.6-1.7l4-3.3c-0.9-1.9-2-3.8-3.2-5.5L69.2,34 c-0.4-0.5-0.8-0.9-1.2-1.3l2.4-4.6c-1.6-1.4-3.3-2.7-5.1-3.8l-3.7,3.6c-0.5-0.3-1.1-0.5-1.6-0.8l0.5-5.2c-2-0.7-4-1.3-6.2-1.6 l-2.1,4.8c-0.6-0.1-1.2-0.1-1.8-0.1l-1.5-5c-2.2,0.1-4.3,0.4-6.3,0.9l-0.1,5.2c-0.6,0.2-1.1,0.4-1.7,0.6l-3.3-4 c-1.9,0.9-3.8,2-5.5,3.2l1.9,4.9c-0.5,0.4-0.9,0.8-1.3,1.2l-4.6-2.4c-1.4,1.6-2.7,3.3-3.8,5.1l3.6,3.7c-0.3,0.5-0.5,1.1-0.8,1.6 l-5.2-0.5c-0.7,2-1.3,4-1.6,6.2l4.8,2.1c-0.1,0.6-0.1,1.2-0.1,1.8l-5,1.5c0.1,2.2,0.4,4.3,0.9,6.3l5.2,0.1c0.2,0.6,0.4,1.1,0.6,1.7 l-4,3.3c0.9,1.9,2,3.8,3.2,5.5l4.9-1.9c0.4,0.5,0.8,0.9,1.2,1.3l-2.4,4.6c1.6,1.4,3.3,2.7,5.1,3.8l3.7-3.6c0.5,0.3,1.1,0.5,1.6,0.8 l-0.5,5.2c2,0.7,4,1.3,6.2,1.6l2.1-4.8c0.6,0.1,1.2,0.1,1.8,0.1l1.5,5c2.2-0.1,4.3-0.4,6.3-0.9l0.1-5.2c0.6-0.2,1.1-0.4,1.7-0.6 l3.3,4c1.9-0.9,3.8-2,5.5-3.2L66,69.2c0.5-0.4,0.9-0.8,1.3-1.2l4.6,2.4c1.4-1.6,2.7-3.3,3.8-5.1l-3.6-3.7c0.3-0.5,0.5-1.1,0.8-1.6 l5.2,0.5c0.7-2,1.3-4,1.6-6.2l-4.8-2.1C74.9,51.7,75,51.1,75,50.5z M50,65c-8.3,0-15-6.7-15-15c0-8.3,6.7-15,15-15s15,6.7,15,15 C65,58.3,58.3,65,50,65z" fill="#000000"><animateTransform attributeName="transform" type="rotate" from="0 50 50" to="90 50 50" dur="3s" repeatCount="indefinite"></animateTransform></path></svg>')) : ""
        
    ///////////////
                
    },

    errorView: function(e) {
        return e ? m(".error", "konnte keine Verbindung mit der Datenbank herstellen…") : null
    }
}

var docsetted = !!app.doc()
var besetztsetted = !!app.besetzt()
var hash = "5d44d376cd42118ec5849913521fb728"

m.route(document.body, "/", {
    "/":       { onmatch: function(resolve, args, requestedPath) {   m.route.set("/start") }},
    "/opernblog": { onmatch: function(resolve, args, requestedPath) { 
                     app.sparte("oper")
                     app.spartenclass("oper")
                     app.blogdoc = {}
                     app.searchresult = []
                     ga('send', 'pageview', requestedPath)
                     if(mobilenavopen) animatenav(1)
                     docsetted = false
                     besetztsetted = false
                     m.request({ method: 'GET', url: 'http://buehnen-halle.de/x/opernblog' })
                     .run(function(r){ 
                         app.doc({slug: "opernblog", sorte:"opernblog", _id:r.doc[0].id, _rev:r.doc[0].rev, kaestchen: !!r.doc[0].kaestchen ? JSON.parse(r.doc[0].kaestchen) : null})        
                         app.blogdoc = {last5:r.last5, tags: r.tags}
                         
                         })
                     resolve(app); }, 
                  render: function(vnode) { vnode.key = Math.random(); return vnode} },
 
    "/opernblog/tags/:tag": { onmatch: function(resolve, args, requestedPath) { 
                     console.log(requestedPath)
                     app.searchresult = []
                     ga('send', 'pageview', requestedPath)
                     if(mobilenavopen) animatenav(1)
                     m.request({ method: 'GET', url: 'http://buehnen-halle.de/x/opernblog/tags/' + args.tag })
                     .run(function(r){ 
                         app.blogdoc = {posts:r.posts, tags: r.tags}
                         app.doc({sorte:"opernblog"})                         
                         app.sparte("oper")
                         app.spartenclass("oper")
                         })
                     resolve(app); }, 
                  render: function(vnode) { vnode.key = Math.random(); return vnode} },
    
     "/opernblog/eintrag/:id": { onmatch: function(resolve, args, requestedPath) { 
                    app.searchresult = []
                     ga('send', 'pageview', requestedPath)
                     if(mobilenavopen) animatenav(1)
                    m.request({ method: 'GET', url: 'http://buehnen-halle.de/x/opernblog/eintrag/' + args.id })
                    .run(function(r){ 
                        var post = r.post[0]
                        app.blogdoc = {post:post, tags: r.tags}
                        app.doc({sorte:post.sorte, tags: post.tags, autor: post.autor, teaser: post.teaser,  _id:post.id, _rev:post.rev, titel: post.titel, text:post.text, erzeugt: post.erzeugt, update: post.geändert, kaestchen: !!post.kaestchen ? JSON.parse(post.kaestchen) : null}) 
                        app.sparte("oper")
                        app.spartenclass("oper")
                        })
                    resolve(app); }, 
                 render: function(vnode) { vnode.key = Math.random(); return vnode} },
                        
    "/:seite": { onmatch: function(resolve, args, requestedPath) { 
                    if(/presse/.test(requestedPath) && requestedPath != "/presse" && md5(app.pressepass) != hash) { if(md5(app.pressepass) != hash)  { app.pressepass = prompt("Passwort für den Pressebereich:"); }}
                    ga('send', 'pageview', requestedPath)
                    if(mobilenavopen) animatenav(1)
                    app.searchresult = []
                    app.blogdoc = {}
                    docsetted = false
                    if(!(/presse/.test(requestedPath) && requestedPath != "/presse" && md5(app.pressepass) != hash)) {
                    var req = !docsetted ? m.request({ method: 'GET', url: 'http://buehnen-halle.de/x/seite' + requestedPath }) : app.doc 
                    app.doc = req.run(function(r){return r.rows[0] ? r.rows[0].doc : null; }) }
                    var req2 = !besetztsetted ? m.request({ method: 'GET', url: 'http://buehnen-halle.de/x/besetzt/17' + requestedPath }) : app.besetzt
                    besetztsetted = false
                    app.besetzt = req2.run(function(r){return !!r.rows ? unique(r.rows.map(function(b){return b.value}),"kuerzel") : null; });
                    app.sparte = req.run(function(r){var doc = r.rows[0].doc; return (!!doc.sparte && !!doc.sparte[0] ? doc.sparte[0].toLowerCase() : null)});
                    app.spartenclass = req.run(function(r){var doc = r.rows[0].doc; return (!!doc.sparte && !!doc.sparte[0] ? doc.sparte[0].toLowerCase().replace(/ /g,"_").replace(/\//g,"") : null) + " " + (!!doc.slug ? doc.slug : null)});     
                    app.bilderstrecke([]); 
                    resolve(app); }, 
                 render: function(vnode) { vnode.key = Math.random(); return vnode} }
});

m.route.prefix("")


 

    
    
</script>
</body>
</html>
